Senvr: '`; hello-DOS.asm - single-segment, 16-bit "hello world" program
;
; assemble with "nasm -f bin -o hi.com hello-DOS.asm"

    org  0x100        ; .com files always start 256 bytes into the segment

    ; int 21h is going to want...

    mov  dx, msg      ; the address of or message in dx
    mov  ah, 9        ; ah=9 - "print string" sub-function
    int  0x21         ; call dos services

    mov  ah, 0x4c     ; "terminate program" sub-function
    int  0x21         ; call dos services

    msg  db 'Hello, World!', 0x0d, 0x0a, '$'   ; $-terminated message`'

Senvr: '`def isSudoer(person, ctx):
    print(str(ctx.message.server.id)+"/sudoers.conf")
    print("A")
    if not Path(str(ctx.message.server.id)+"/sudoers.conf").exists():
        os.mkdir(str(ctx.message.server.id))
        open(str(ctx.message.server.id)+"/sudoers.conf","x")
    sudofile=open(str(ctx.message.server.id)+"/sudoers.conf","r")
    regex = re.compile('[^0-9]')
    sudoers=sudofile.read().strip().split()
    sudofile.close
    print(sudoers)
    owner=ctx.message.server.owner.id
    print("B")
    
    sudoRole=fileVarRead(ctx, "sudo-role")
    if not sudoRole == "":
        for y in ctx.message.server.get_member(person).roles:
            if sudoRole in str(y.id).strip().lower():
                print("MATCH")
                print(str(person)+" is a sudoer. They have the role.")
                return True
            else:
                print("looking for "+sudoRole+" in "+y.id)
    if person == owner:
        print(str(person)+" is the owner.")
        return True;
    elif person in sudoers:
        print(str(person)+" is a sudoer.")
        return True;
    else:
        print(str(person)+" is not a sudoer.")
        return False;`'

Senvr: '```@bot.command(pass_context=True)
async def changevar(ctx, name, value):
    if isSudoer(str(ctx.message.author.id),ctx) == True:
        name=str(name).lower().strip()
        print(name)
        value=str(value).lower().strip()
        await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Attempting to change variable "+name+" with value "+value)
        if name == "main-general":
            fileVarWrite(ctx, name, value)
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Wrote changes. Re-reading the value: ")
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, fileVarRead(ctx, name))
            return;
        elif name == "pending-role":
            fileVarWrite(ctx, name, value)
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Wrote changes. Re-reading the value: ")
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, fileVarRead(ctx, name))
            return;
        elif name == "frame-role":
            fileVarWrite(ctx, name, value)
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Wrote changes. Re-reading the value: ")
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, fileVarRead(ctx, name))
            return;    
        elif name == "results-channel":
            fileVarWrite(ctx, name, value)
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Wrote changes. Re-reading the value: ")
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, fileVarRead(ctx, name))
            return;    
        elif name == "sudo-role":
            fileVarWrite(ctx, name, value)
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "Wrote changes. Re-reading the value: ")
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, fileVarRead(ctx, name))
            return;    
            
        else:
            await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "ERROR: 404")
    else:
        await bot.send_message(ctx.message.channel, "ERROR: 401")```'

#include "stdlib.h"
#include "stdio.h"

int main(int argc, char** argv){
    if(argc < 2){
        printf("Usage: %s <num1> [num2] [...]\n", argv[0]);
        return -1;
    }
    float res = 0;
    for(int i = 1; i < argc; i++)
